statute prohemium iohannis rastell lawys real • eglōd wel statute iug • mētis decreys made wrytyn cōmynly frēche tōge dyuerse men thereof muse haue oft tymys cōmunicaciō argumēte cōsyderīg reason euery law wherto people shuld bo •• dyn oughte shuld wrytt • n suche maner opynly publyssed decl •• yd people myght sone without gret di • ficulte haue knowlege thesame lawes cause whithe said lawes ēglōd writī frēch tōg shuld seme fyrste vnknowyn wyllyam duke normandy came lande slewe kyng herrold conqueryd hole realm great nōbre people wel gentilmē cam vnderstode vulgar tong tyme vsyd realme onely frēch tōg also cause sayd kyng great wyse mē coū sel ꝑseiuid supposid vulgar tōg w • ich vsyd realme maner homely rude greate copy ād • aboundaūce wordys frenche tōg thā 〈◊〉 • vullgare tonge sel • suffycyent expound declare matter lawis ordenaūcꝭ thei hade determine • made good gouernaūce people effectually substauncyally cowd indyte thē frēch tong therfore order • wrote indited seid law made french tong forthermore longe cōmyng kynge wylyā conquerour yt vse frēch tōg ī real began mynyssh dyuers people thā inhabytyd withī realm coud nother speke vulgare tongue realme nother french tong therfore wyse men realme causyd orderyd matter law accyōs betwene ꝑtes shuld pledyd shewyd defendyd answered debatyd • • uggyd englyssh vulgar tōg ouer y• wryttyn enteryd recorde rollys latyn tonge cause euery man generally • indyfferently myght haue knowlege thereof apperyth statute made xxxvi yere ed iii ca vltimo wherefore suppose causꝭ rehersyd law realm īdytid wryttī frēch tōg ītēdyd ryght good purpose yet besyde late day moste noble prynce late souereyn lorde kynge henry vii worthye called seconde salomon whiche excellyd polytyk wysedome pryncis reyngned realm tyme concyderynge well perseyuynge vulgare englissh tong maruelously amendyd augmentyd reason dyuerse famous clerkys lernyd men translate made many noble workys englisshe tōg wherby moch plenty haboundan̄ce englyssh vsyd tymys past reasō ther vulgare tōg āplified sufficient self expound lawys ordinaūcis nedeful made ordre realm also thesame wyse price consyderyng vnyuersall people realm greate pleasure gaue thēself greatly redynge vulgare englyssh tonge ordeynyd causyd statutys ordinauncis made commyn welth realm dayes shulde indytyd wryttyn vulgare englyssh tonge publysshyd declaryd imprītid thā vnyuersally people realm myght sone haue knowleg sayd statutꝭ ordynaū cys bound obserue reasō knowlege auoid daūger • penaltes statutys also better lyffe tranquylyte pea dyscreyt charytable resonable order drad souereyne lord kyng henry viii hath cō tynuyd folowyd causyd statutys haue made dayes also īdytyd wrytten englyssh tonge intente lege people might haue knowleg ther goodly purposys intentys mynde oftē tymys reuoluyde hath causyd • ake lytell payne translate frenche englysshe abbreuyacyon statutys •• fyrst yere reyn late • uereyn lord kyng
